这是一种民间艺术，在20世纪60年代和70年代，在田的家乡宁夏回族自治区同心县非常流行。
It ' s a kind of folk art that was very popular in Tian ' s hometown , Tongxin county , Northwest China ' s Ningxia Hui autonomous region , during the 1960s and ' 70s .

早在2001年，中国农民艺术中心就已在秀洲区成立，此后每两到三年举办一次农民绘画节。
Starting as early as 2001 , the China Farmers Art Center was already established in Xiuzhou district , and a festival featuring farmers paintings has been held every two to three years since then .

“康卫华”的字面意思是“床周围的画”，在当地方言中，“康”是一种加热床的名称。
Kangweihua literally means " paintings around bed " , with kang being the name of a kind of heated bed in the local dialect .

8月15日，上海奉贤博物馆举办了一场名为“无限如天——周秦汉唐珍宝”的展览，展览将持续到9月15日。
An exhibition titled Infinite Like Heavens – Treasures from Zhou , Qin Han and Tang Dynasties kicked off at Shanghai Fengxian Museum on August 15 and will last until September 15 .
7月15日，上海奉贤博物馆举办了一场名为“无限如天——周秦汉唐珍宝”的展览，展览将持续到9月15日。
An exhibition titled Infinite Like Heavens – Treasures from Zhou , Qin Han and Tang Dynasties kicked off at Shanghai Fengxian Museum on July 15 and will last until September 15 .

An exhibition entitled Infinite Like Heavens – Treasures from Zhou , Qin Han and Tang Dynasties kicked off at Shanghai Fengxian Museum on July 15 and will last until September 15 .

Fascinated by all kinds of knowledge from a young age , he became a docent at the NMC more than 20 years ago after graduating from university , where he majored in computer science .
